              <div data-v-e187e7b6="" class="doc-title-box"><span data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title-span"
                  class="dn"></span>
                <h2 data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title">gb-drawer 抽屉</h2>
              </div>
              <div data-v-e5df71aa="" data-v-e187e7b6="" id="editor-md"
                class="main-editor markdown-body editormd-html-preview">
                <link data-v-e5df71aa="" href="static/editor.md/css/editormd.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
                <!---->
                <h3 id="h3-u6982u8FF0"><a name="概述" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>概述</h3>
                <p>iview中 Drawer 组件的扩展，增加全屏扩展的功能，<a href="https://run.iviewui.com/vGKAZUps" title="查看Demo"
                    target="_blank">查看Demo</a>,效果图如下：</p>
                <p><img src="http://help.op110.com.cn/server/../Public/Uploads/2018-12-17/5c17a72d4b1bf.gif" alt=""></p>
                <h3 id="h3-u4F7Fu7528"><a name="使用" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>使用</h3>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">import</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">GbDrawer</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">from</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">'_c/drawer'</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">export</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">default</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    components</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        </span><span class="typ">GbDrawer</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pun">}</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="tag">&lt;gb-drawer&gt;&lt;/gb-drawer&gt;</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <h3 id="h3-api"><a name="API" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>API</h3>
                <blockquote>
                  <p>API基本同 iview中的 Drawer组件一致，在其基础上新增 <code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">expandable</code>
                    属性控制展开按钮的显隐，<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">on-expand-change</code>事件监听展开/收起的回调，并移除<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">mask-closable</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">mask</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">mask-style</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">transfer</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">class-name</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">inner</code>等属性</p>
                </blockquote>
                <h4 id="h4-props-"><a name="Props 属性" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Props 属性</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">属性</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">类型</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">默认值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>value</td>
                        <td>抽屉是否显示，可使用 v-model 双向绑定数据</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>title</td>
                        <td>抽屉标题，如果使用 slot 自定义了页头，则 title 无效</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>width</td>
                        <td>抽屉宽度。当其值不大于 100 时以百分比显示，大于 100 时为像素</td>
                        <td>Number ¦ String</td>
                        <td>600</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>closable</td>
                        <td>是否显示右上角的关闭按钮</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>true</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>styles</td>
                        <td>抽屉中间层的样式</td>
                        <td>Object</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>scrollable</td>
                        <td>页面是否可以滚动</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>false</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>placement</td>
                        <td>抽屉的方向，可选值为 left 或 right</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>right</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>expandable</td>
                        <td>是否显示右上角可展开的按钮</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>false</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
                <h4 id="h4-events-"><a name="Events 事件" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Events 事件</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">事件名</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">返回值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>on-close</td>
                        <td>关闭抽屉时触发</td>
                        <td>无</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>on-visible-change</td>
                        <td>显示状态发生变化时触发</td>
                        <td>true / false</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>on-expand-change</td>
                        <td>抽屉扩展/收缩时触发</td>
                        <td>true / false</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
                <h4 id="h4-slot-"><a name="Slot 插槽" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Slot 插槽</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">名称</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>header</td>
                        <td>自定义标题栏</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>footer</td>
                        <td>自定义底部栏</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>close</td>
                        <td>显示状态发生变化时触发</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>默认</td>
                        <td>抽屉主体内容</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
              </div>

                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>概述</h3>
                <p>iview中 Button 组件的扩展，增加点击水波纹特效，效果如下图：<br><img
                    src="http://help.op110.com.cn/server/../Public/Uploads/2018-12-17/5c17a59ccfb16.gif" alt=""></p>

                <h2 data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title">department-selector-modal 部门选择弹框</h2>
              </div>
              <div data-v-e5df71aa="" data-v-e187e7b6="" id="editor-md"
                class="main-editor markdown-body editormd-html-preview">
                <link data-v-e5df71aa="" href="static/editor.md/css/editormd.min.css" rel="stylesheet">

                <h3 id="h3-u6982u8FF0"><a name="概述" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>概述</h3>
                <p><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">DepartmentSelectorModal</code>属于全局业务组件，所以文件路径为<code
                    style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">src/view/components/department-selector-modal</code>，组件用于选择公司部门，可以单选或多选，效果图如下：
                </p>
                <p><img src="http://help.op110.com.cn/server/../Public/Uploads/2018-12-17/5c17a7ee3319d.gif" alt=""></p>
                <h3 id="h3-u4F7Fu7528"><a name="使用" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>使用</h3>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">import</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">DepartmentSelectorModal</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">from</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">'@/view/components/department-selector-modal'</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">export</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">default</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    components</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        </span><span class="typ">DepartmentSelectorModal</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pun">}</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    :</span><span class="atn">operate-data</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none;                 <h3 id="h3-api"><a name="API" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>API</h3>
                <blockquote>
                  <p>API基本同 iview中的 Drawer组件一致，在其基础上新增 <code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">expandable</code>
                    属性控制展开按钮的显隐，<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">on-expand-change</code>事件监听展开/收起的回调，并移除<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">mask-closable</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">mask</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">mask-style</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">transfer</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">class-name</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">inner</code>等属性</p>
                </blockquote>
                <h4 id="h4-props-"><a name="Props 属性" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Props 属性</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">属性</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">类型</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">默认值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>value</td>
                        <td>弹窗是否显示，可使用 v-model 双向绑定数据</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>title</td>
                        <td>弹窗标题标题</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>选择部门</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>multiple</td>
                        <td>是否可以多选</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>false</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>operate-data</td>
                        <td>选中的员工数据，主要用于批量修改员工部门，不用可不设置</td>
                        <td>Array</td>
                        <td>[]</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>selected-data</td>
                        <td>已选择的部门数据，类型为Array，Array的值为Object，Object必须包含部门id，部门名称，部门路径，例如：<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">[{id: 1, name: '研发部', deptPath: '[1,2]' }]</code></td>
                        <td>Array</td>
                        <td>[]</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
                <h4 id="h4-events-"><a name="Events 事件" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Events 事件</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">事件名</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">返回值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>on-change</td>
                        <td>选择部门完成后触发</td>
                        <td>Array，已选部门数据</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>on-success</td>
                        <td>批量更新成员成功后触发</td>
                        <td>—</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
              </div>

                <h3 id="h3-u6982u8FF0"><a name="概述" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>概述</h3>
                <p>配合iview跑马灯实现图片预览，组件存放路径 <code
                    style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">src/view/components/gb-view-image</code></p>
                <h3 id="h3--"><a name="使用方式 (已注册全局组件)" class="reference-link"></a><span

                <h3 id="h3-props-"><a name="props 属性" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>props 属性</h3>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">

                        <th style="width: 180px;">类型</th>

                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>interval</td>
                        <td>自动播放间隔时间</td>
                        <td>Number</td>
                        <td>3000</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>value</td>
                        <td>控制显示或隐藏，可用v-model</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>false</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>view-value</td>
                        <td>从索引开始显示图片</td>
                        <td>number</td>
                        <td>0</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>toolbar</td>
                        <td>是否在顶部显示title</td>
                        <td>[Boolean, Number]</td>
                        <td>true</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>title</td>
                        <td>图片名字显示</td>
                        <td>[Boolean, Number]</td>
                        <td>true</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>navbar</td>
                        <td>导航栏显示</td>
                        <td>[Boolean, Number]</td>
                        <td>true</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>minZoomRatio</td>
                        <td>最小缩放比例</td>
                        <td>Number</td>
                        <td>0.1</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>

                <h3 id="h3-event-"><a name="event 事件" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>event 事件</h3>

                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>on-close</td>
                        <td>关闭右上角事件</td>
                        <td>图片组件实例</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>on-change</td>
                        <td>切换图片时触发，激活的索引，原索引，当前data对象，图片实例</td>
                        <td>oldValue, value, itme, this</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>

                <h2 data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title">gb-pulldown-drawer 全局下拉抽屉</h2>

                <h3 id="h3-u6982u8FF0"><a name="概述" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>概述</h3>
                <p>全局下拉抽屉，主要使用在系统头部，点击头部导航或按钮下拉展开面板，效果图如下：</p>
                <p><img src="http://help.op110.com.cn/server/../Public/Uploads/2018-12-17/5c17a9d702410.gif" alt=""></p>
                <h3 id="h3-u4F7Fu7528"><a name="使用" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>使用</h3>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">import</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">GbPulldownDrawer</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">from</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">'_c/pulldown-drawer'</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">export</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">default</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    components</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        </span><span class="typ">GbPulldownDrawer</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pun">}</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="tag">&lt;gb-pulldown-drawer</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">v-model</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span><span class="pln"> @</span><span class="atn">on-change</span><span class="tag">&gt;&lt;/gb-pulldown-drawer&gt;</span></code></li></ol></pre>

                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>API</h3>

                        <th style="width: 180px;">类型</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">默认值</th>

                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">

                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>false</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>

                <h4 id="h4-events-"><a name="Events 事件" class="reference-link"></a><span

                      </tr>
                    </thead>

                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">

                        <td>true/false</td>
                      </tr>

                  </table>

                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>header</td>
                        <td>添加头部内容，头部高度固定为 50px</td>
                      </tr>

              <div data-v-e187e7b6="" class="doc-title-box"><span data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title-span"
                  class="dn"></span>
                <h2 data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title">preset-avatar 预设默认头像</h2>
              </div>
              <div data-v-e5df71aa="" data-v-e187e7b6="" id="editor-md"
                class="main-editor markdown-body editormd-html-preview">
                <link data-v-e5df71aa="" href="static/editor.md/css/editormd.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
                <!---->
                <h3 id="h3-u6982u8FF0"><a name="概述" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>概述</h3>
                <p><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">PresetAvatar</code>属于全局业务组件，所以文件路径为<code
                    style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">src/view/components/preset-avatar</code>，组件用于显示用户默认头像，如下图：<br><img
                    src="http://help.op110.com.cn/server/../Public/Uploads/2018-12-17/5c17a34fe2456.png" alt=""></p>
                <h3 id="h3-u4F7Fu7528"><a name="使用" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>使用</h3>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">import</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">PresetAvatar</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">from</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">'@/view/components/preset-avatar'</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">export</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">default</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    components</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        </span><span class="typ">PresetAvatar</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pun">}</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="tag">&lt;preset-avatar</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    :</span><span class="atn">user-id</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    :</span><span class="atn">size</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    :</span><span class="atn">shape</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    :</span><span class="atn">src</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="tag">&gt;</span><span class="pln">用户名称</span><span class="tag">&lt;/preset-avatar&gt;</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <h3 id="h3-api"><a name="API" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>API</h3>
                <blockquote>
                  <p>API基本同 iview中的 Drawer组件一致，在其基础上新增 <code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">expandable</code>
                    属性控制展开按钮的显隐，<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">on-expand-change</code>事件监听展开/收起的回调，并移除<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">mask-closable</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">mask</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">mask-style</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">transfer</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">class-name</code>、<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">inner</code>等属性</p>
                </blockquote>
                <h4 id="h4-props-"><a name="Props 属性" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Props 属性</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">属性</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">类型</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">默认值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>user-id</td>
                        <td>用户id ，需要根据用户id随机生成背景颜色</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>size</td>
                        <td>设置头像的大小，自定义指定数值</td>
                        <td>Number</td>
                        <td>32</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>shape</td>
                        <td>指定头像的形状，可选值为 circle、square</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>circle</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>src</td>
                        <td>图片类头像的资源地址</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
                <h4 id="h4-slot-"><a name="Slot 插槽" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Slot 插槽</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">名称</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>close</td>
                        <td>删除头像</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>无</td>
                        <td>用户名称</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>

              <div data-v-e187e7b6="" class="doc-title-box"><span data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title-span"
                  class="dn"></span>
                <h2 data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title">people-select-modal 成员选择弹窗</h2>
              </div>
              <div data-v-e5df71aa="" data-v-e187e7b6="" id="editor-md"
                class="main-editor markdown-body editormd-html-preview">
                <link data-v-e5df71aa="" href="static/editor.md/css/editormd.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
                <!---->
                <h3 id="h3-u6982u8FF0"><a name="概述" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>概述</h3>
                <p><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">PeopleSelectModal</code>属于全局业务组件，所以文件路径为<code
                    style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">src/view/components/people-select-modal</code>，组件可根据当前企业的组织架构、成员角色、我的部门选择企业成员，效果如下图：
                </p>
                <p><img src="http://help.op110.com.cn/server/../Public/Uploads/2018-12-17/5c179d3bea3d9.gif" alt=""></p>
                <h3 id="h3-u4F7Fu7528"><a name="使用" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>使用</h3>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">import</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">PeopleSelectModal</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">from</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">'@/view/components/people-select-modal'</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">export</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">default</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    components</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        </span><span class="typ">PeopleSelectModal</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pun">}</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="tag">&lt;people-select-modal</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="atn">v-model</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    :</span><span class="atn">max</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    :</span><span class="atn">tabs</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    :</span><span class="atn">selected-data</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    @</span><span class="atn">on-ok</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">""</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="tag">&lt;/people-select-modal&gt;</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <h4 id="h4-props-"><a name="Props 属性" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Props 属性</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">属性</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">类型</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">默认值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>value</td>
                        <td>显示对话框，可使用<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">v-model</code>进行双向板顶</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>false</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>max</td>
                        <td>可选成员数量最大限制，最大值为<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">1000</code>,最小值为<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">1</code>, 等于<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">1</code>时触发单选操作</td>
                        <td>Number</td>
                        <td>50</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>departmentId</td>
                        <td>部门id，仅用于选择当前部门所有成员</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>tabs</td>
                        <td>tab选项卡个数和显隐配置，<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">departmentId</code>存在时，配置将失效</td>
                        <td>Array</td>
                        <td>[‘department’, ‘role’, ‘myDepartment’]</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>selecteData</td>
                        <td>读取已选成员,成员值必须包含<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">id/name/avatar</code>字段</td>
                        <td>Array</td>
                        <td>[]</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
                <h4 id="h4-event-"><a name="Event 事件" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Event 事件</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">名称</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">返回值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>on-ok</td>
                        <td>选择成员成功后的回调</td>
                        <td>Array 已选成员</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
              </div>

                <h3 id="h3-u6982u8FF0"><a name="概述" class="reference-link"></a><span

                <h4 id="h4--strong-view-model-strong-"><a
                    name="<strong>view-model组件，主要使用在各列表展示模块，用户可根据视图的配置，展示不同的数据：</strong>"
                    class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span><strong>view-model组件，主要使用在各列表展示模块，用户可根据视图的配置，展示不同的数据：</strong>

            <main data-v-e187e7b6="" class="el-main page_content_main" id="page_content_main">
              <div data-v-e187e7b6="" class="doc-title-box"><span data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title-span"
                  class="dn"></span>
                <h2 data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title">iv-grid 网格组件</h2>
              </div>
              <div data-v-e5df71aa="" data-v-e187e7b6="" id="editor-md"
                class="main-editor markdown-body editormd-html-preview">
                <link data-v-e5df71aa="" href="static/editor.md/css/editormd.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
                <!---->
                <h3 id="h3-u6982u8FF0"><a name="概述" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>概述</h3>
                <p>由于iview中 <code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">Table</code>
                  组件在渲染可编辑form表单时，添加或删除列，会重新渲染整个表格，故扩展该组件；<code
                    style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">iv-grid</code>组件布局主要依赖iview的<code
                    style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">Row</code>和<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">Col</code>组件;
                  编辑模式下，支持键盘<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">tab</code>、<code
                    style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">left</code>、<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">up</code>、<code
                    style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">right</code>、<code
                    style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">down</code>切换表单焦点</p>
                <h3 id="h3-u5B9Eu73B0u529Fu80FD"><a name="实现功能" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>实现功能</h3>
                <ul>
                  <li>宽度不够，自动补宽</li>
                  <li>左右固定列</li>
                  <li>选择行</li>
                  <li>高亮行</li>
                  <li>表单验证</li>
                  <li>tab键切换</li>
                  <li>上下左右按键切换</li>
                  <li>新增空状态（可配置描述+文字）</li>
                </ul>
                <h3 id="h3-u4F7Fu7528"><a name="使用" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>使用</h3>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">import</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="typ">IvGrid</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">from</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">'_c/grid'</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">export</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">default</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    components</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        </span><span class="typ">IvGrid</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pun">}</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="tag">&lt;iv-grid&gt;&lt;/iv-grid&gt;</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <h3 id="h3-api"><a name="API" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>API</h3>
                <blockquote>
                  <p>注意：<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">iv-grid</code>网格默认为预览状态，编辑状态需要手动通过<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">scope-slot</code>作用域插槽手动配置；</p>
                </blockquote>
                <h4 id="h4-props-"><a name="Props 属性" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Props 属性</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">属性</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">类型</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">默认值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>data</td>
                        <td>显示的结构化数据</td>
                        <td>Array</td>
                        <td>[]</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>columns</td>
                        <td>网格列的配置选项，详细配置参数，请查看<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">column</code>配置</td>
                        <td>Array</td>
                        <td>[]</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>stripe</td>
                        <td>是否显示间隔斑马纹</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>true</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>show-header</td>
                        <td>是否显示网格头部</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>true</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>loading</td>
                        <td>表格是否加载中</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>false</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>empty</td>
                        <td>数据为空状态时，自定义描述内容和图片</td>
                        <td>String ¦ Object</td>
                        <td>暂无数据</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>highlight-row</td>
                        <td>高亮行的回调方法：<br> 传入参数：<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">index</code>:当前行索引；<br>返回值：高亮行的样式名称</td>
                        <td>Function</td>
                        <td>‘’</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
                <h4 id="h4-events-"><a name="Events 事件" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Events 事件</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">事件名</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">返回值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>on-row-delete</td>
                        <td>删除行</td>
                        <td><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">row</code>: 当前被删除的行<br><code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">index</code>：当前被删除行的索引</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>on-select</td>
                        <td>在<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">selection</code>模式下有效，选中某一行或多行时触发</td>
                        <td>Array：已选的<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">row</code>的集合</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
                <h4 id="h4-methods-"><a name="Methods 方法" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Methods 方法</h4>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">方法名</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">返回值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>validate</td>
                        <td>编辑状态下，对所有表单进行校验</td>
                        <td>Promise，参数为true时，验证成功;<br>为false时，自动获取第一个错误表单元素的焦点</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>resetFields</td>
                        <td>重置表单元素错误提示</td>
                        <td>- </td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>addLinkageValidate</td>
                        <td>添加指定列的联动验证</td>
                        <td>index：当前网格行的索引；<br>keys：Array，联动列的key的集合，</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>removeLinkageValidate</td>
                        <td>移除指定列的联动验证</td>
                        <td>index：当前网格行的索引；<br>keys：Array，被联动列的key的集合</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>addLinkageRequired</td>
                        <td>添加指定列的联动验证必填状态</td>
                        <td>keys：Array，联动列的key的集合，</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>removeLinkageRequired</td>
                        <td>移除指定列的联动验证必填状态</td>
                        <td>keys：Array，被联动列的key的集合</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
                <h4 id="h4-slot-"><a name="Slot 插槽" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>Slot 插槽</h4>
                <h5 id="h5-u5177u540Du63D2u69FD"><a name="具名插槽" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>具名插槽</h5>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">名称</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>loading</td>
                        <td>加载中</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>transfer</td>
                        <td>对需要多次渲染的外部组件提供插槽，可以通过手动监听组件显隐状态，避免多次渲染</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
                <p><strong>通过transfer插槽手动引入iview的datePicker简单实现，具体实现请<a
                      href="http://xqtest.op110.com.cn/examples/grid/transfer" target="_blank">查看demo</a></strong></p>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="kwd">this</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">datePicker</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">colKey </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> key</span></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="kwd">this</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">datePicker</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">rowIndex </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> index</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="kwd">this</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">datePicker</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">left </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> offset</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">left</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="kwd">this</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">datePicker</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">top </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> offset</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">top </span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">40</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">},</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    hideDatePicker </span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L7" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="kwd">this</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">datePicker</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">show </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">false</span></code></li><li class="L8" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">},</span></code></li><li class="L9" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    addRowData </span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      let item </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        startDate</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">'2019-02-27'</span><span class="pun">,</span></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        endDate</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">'2019-05-04'</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="kwd">this</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">gridDatas</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">push</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">item</span><span class="pun">)</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">},</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    submitFormData </span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L7" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="kwd">this</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">$refs</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">gridForm</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">validate</span><span class="pun">().</span><span class="pln">then</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="pln">res </span><span class="pun">=&gt;</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L8" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        console</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">log</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="str">'验证结果：'</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> res</span><span class="pun">)</span></code></li><li class="L9" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="pun">})</span></code></li><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">},</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    resetGridForm </span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="kwd">this</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">$refs</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">gridForm</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">resetFields</span><span class="pun">()</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">  </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="tag">&lt;/script&gt;</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <h5 id="h5-scope-slot-"><a name="scope-slot 作用域插槽" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>scope-slot 作用域插槽</h5>
                <blockquote>
                  <p>列描述数据对象<code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">column</code>中属性包含<code
                      style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">slot</code>时，作用域插槽生效，使用作用域插槽手动配置表格编辑状态：</p>
                </blockquote>
                <p><strong>插槽 props</strong></p>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">属性</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">类型</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">默认值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>row</td>
                        <td>当前操作行数据</td>
                        <td>Object</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>index</td>
                        <td>当前操作行索引</td>
                        <td>Number</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>offset</td>
                        <td>当前操作单元格相对整个grid容器的偏移值；<br><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">offset.left</code>:
                          距离左侧的距离<br><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">offset.top</code>: 距离顶部的距离（包含当前单元格的高度，与<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">getBoundingClientRect.bottom</code>类似）</td>
                        <td>Object</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="tag">&lt;template&gt;</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="tag">&lt;iv-grid:columns</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"columns"</span><span class="pln"> :</span><span class="atn">data</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"data"</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        </span><span class="tag">&lt;template</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">slot-scope</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"{ row, index, offset }"</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="atn">slot</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="atv">"name"</span><span class="tag">&gt;</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">            </span><span class="tag">&lt;strong&gt;</span><span class="pln">{{ row.name }}</span><span class="tag">&lt;/strong&gt;</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">        </span><span class="tag">&lt;/template&gt;</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="tag">&lt;/iv-grid&gt;</span></code></li><li class="L6" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="tag">&lt;/template&gt;</span></code></li></ol></pre>
                <h4 id="h4-column-"><a name="column 配置" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>column 配置</h4>
                <p>列描述数据对象，是 columns 中的一项</p>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <th style="width: 180px;">属性</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">说明</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">类型</th>
                        <th style="width: 180px;">默认值</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>type</td>
                        <td>列类型，可选值为：<br> <code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">index</code>：显示行的序号<br><code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">selection</code>：显示可选择行状态<br><code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">action</code>：操作项，目前只支持删除</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>title</td>
                        <td>列头显示文字</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>key</td>
                        <td>列的字段名称</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>slot</td>
                        <td>列对应的作用域插槽名称</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>required</td>
                        <td>当前列是否为必填项，在编辑状态生效</td>
                        <td>Boolean</td>
                        <td>false</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>rules</td>
                        <td>当前配置列表单验证规则，具体配置查看 <a href="https://github.com/yiminghe/async-validator"
                            target="_blank">async-validator</a>，在编辑状态生效</td>
                        <td>Array</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>linkageRules</td>
                        <td>当前配置列表单的联动验证规则，具体配置同rules，在编辑状态生效，需要手动通过组件实例的<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">addLinkageValidate</code>触发，结合<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">removeLinkageValidate</code>、<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">addLinkageRequired</code>、<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">removeLinkageRequired</code>使用</td>
                        <td>Array</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>width</td>
                        <td>列宽</td>
                        <td>Number</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>minWidth</td>
                        <td>最小列宽</td>
                        <td>Number</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>maxWidth</td>
                        <td>最大列宽</td>
                        <td>Number</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>align</td>
                        <td>对齐方式，可选值为 left 左对齐、right 右对齐和 center 居中对齐</td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>left</td>
                      </tr>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>fixed</td>
                        <td>列是否固定在左侧或者右侧，可选值为 left 左侧和 right 右侧；<br>type为<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">index</code>、<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">selection</code>时默认设置<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">fixed: left</code><br>type为<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">action</code>时默认设置<code
                            style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);">fixed: right</code></td>
                        <td>String</td>
                        <td>-</td>
                      </tr>
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
              </div>

                <h2 data-v-e187e7b6="" id="doc-title">router-view 路由视图页，公共配置模板</h2>
              </div>
              <div data-v-e5df71aa="" data-v-e187e7b6="" id="editor-md"
                class="main-editor markdown-body editormd-html-preview">
                <link data-v-e5df71aa="" href="static/editor.md/css/editormd.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
                <!---->
                <h3 id="h3--"><a name="带详细注释版本，拷贝请使用下面的优化注释版本，继续往下看↓" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>带详细注释版本，拷贝请使用下面的优化注释版本，继续往下看↓</h3>
                <blockquote>
                  <p>注意：该模板使用在主视图页，而非所有的组件<br>主视图页：顶部标签导航对应的主组件</p>
                </blockquote>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="kwd">export</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">default</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L7" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">  name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">'componentName'</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="com">// 组件名称</span></code></li><li class="L8" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">  inject</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">[</span><span class="str">'app'</span><span class="pun">],</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="com">// 插入全局配置对象</span></code></li><li class="L9" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">  data </span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="kwd">return</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      </span><span class="com">// 当前视图页中的加载状态，在切换标签页时，将影响全局加载状态 this.app.common.pageLoading</span></code></li><li class="L2" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">      currentPageLoading</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">true</span></code></li><li class="L3" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="pun">}</span></code></li><li class="L4" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">  </span><span class="pun">},</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">  </span><span class="pun">},</span></code></li><li class="L8" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">  </span><span class="com">// 切换标签页时触发该钩子</span></code></li><li class="L9" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">  activated </span><span class="pun">()</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">{</span></code></li><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="kwd">this</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">app</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">common</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">pageLoading </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="kwd">this</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">currentPageLoading</span></code></li><li class="L1" style="list-style-type: none;                 <p>欢迎来到同天下文档中心！</p>
                <h3 id="h3-u6982u8FF0"><a name="概述" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>概述</h3>
                <p>搜索下拉关键词高亮组件，如图<br><img
                    src="http://help.op110.com.cn/server/../Public/Uploads/2018-12-01/5c02626d0c7e6.png" alt=""></p>
                <h3 id="h3--"><a name="使用方式 (已注册全局组件)" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>使用方式 (已注册全局组件)</h3>
                <pre class="prettyprint linenums prettyprinted"
                  style="padding-left: 5px; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252); border: 1px solid rgb(225, 225, 232);"><ol class="linenums" style="padding-left: 5px;"><li class="L0" style="list-style-type: none; background-color: rgb(252, 252, 252);"><code style="color: rgb(221, 17, 68);"><span class="pln">    </span><span class="lit">@on</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln">item</span><span class="pun">-</span><span class="pln">click</span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="str">"selectInputItem"</span></code></li><li class="L5" style="list-style-type: none;                 <h3 id="h3-props-"><a name="props 属性" class="reference-link"></a><span
                    class="header-link octicon octicon-link"></span>props 属性</h3>
                <div style="width: 100%;overflow-x: auto;">
                  <table>
                    <thead>
                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(64, 158, 255); color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">

                      <tr style="background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                        <td>itemlist</td>
                        <td>存放搜索结果数组</td>
